--></section><app-seo-data _ngcontent-bbs-c106="" _nghost-bbs-c93="" id="cmsContent"><!-- --><div _ngcontent-bbs-c93="" class="ng-col-12 cms-container ng-star-inserted" id="cms-local-info" inviewport=""><h2 _ngcontent-bbs-c93="" class="header">Buy an Online or Technology Business</h2><div _ngcontent-bbs-c93="" class="content"><div _ngcontent-bbs-c93="" class="info"><div _ngcontent-bbs-c93="" class="ng-star-inserted"><p>E-commerce businesses sell products and services online and operate in a variety of market segments. The industry has reshaped the way businesses operate and consumers shop. In the United States, online and technology companies have experienced exponential growth, becoming a vital part of the economy. E-commerce has allowed small businesses to reach a broader audience, with accessible platforms for their products and services.
</p>
<p>The online and technology industry is constantly changing and expanding and offers numerous benefits to entrepreneurs. With a wide reach, this sector includes businesses in the retail industry with cell phone and computer repair shops to the service industry with software development and graphic design services. E-commerce, online, and technology companies encompass a vast ecosystem of businesses, marketplaces, and platforms that facilitate the buying and selling of goods and services. From the lower barrier to entry and flexibility to diverse revenue streams, e-commerce businesses comprise a wide range of subcategories that include:
</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.bizbuysell.com/cell-phone-and-computer-repair-and-service-businesses-for-sale/">Cell Phone and Computer Repair and Service Businesses</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.bizbuysell.com/graphic-and-web-design-businesses-for-sale/">Graphic Design and Web Design Services</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.bizbuysell.com/it-and-software-service-businesses-for-sale/">IT and Software Service Businesses</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.bizbuysell.com/software-and-app-companies-for-sale/">Software and App Companies</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.bizbuysell.com/websites-and-ecommerce-businesses-for-sale/">Websites and E-Commerce Companies</a></li>
</ul>
<h3>Pricing and Valuation Trends</h3>
<p>Valuations of online and technology businesses vary depending on the category of services and local markets. Overall, trends for the sector show these businesses remain popular options for acquisition. With over 60% growth over the last five years, the average sale price for e-commerce and technology businesses in 2023 was $850,000.
</p>

In the United States, online and technology companies have experienced exponential growth, becoming a vital part of the economy. E-commerce has allowed small businesses to reach a broader audience, with accessible platforms for their products and services.\n&l;/p&g;\n&l;p&g;The online and technology industry is constantly changing and expanding and offers numerous benefits to entrepreneurs. With a wide reach, this sector includes businesses in the retail industry with cell phone and computer repair shops to the service industry with software development and graphic design services. E-commerce, online, and technology companies encompass a vast ecosystem of businesses, marketplaces, and platforms that facilitate the buying and selling of goods and services. From the lower barrier to entry and flexibility to diverse revenue streams, e-commerce businesses comprise a wide range of subcategories that include:\n&l;/p&g;\n&l;ul&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/cell-phone-and-computer-repair-and-service-businesses-for-sale/\&q;&g;Cell Phone and Computer Repair and Service Businesses&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/graphic-and-web-design-businesses-for-sale/\&q;&g;Graphic Design and Web Design Services&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/it-and-software-service-businesses-for-sale/\&q;&g;IT and Software Service Businesses&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/software-and-app-companies-for-sale/\&q;&g;Software and App Companies&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/websites-and-ecommerce-businesses-for-sale/\&q;&g;Websites and E-Commerce Companies&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;\n&l;h3&g;Pricing and Valuation Trends&l;/h3&g;\n&l;p&g;Valuations of online and technology businesses vary depending on the category of services and local markets. Overall, trends for the sector show these businesses remain popular options for acquisition. With over 60% growth over the last five years, the average sale price for e-commerce and technology businesses in 2023 was $850,000.\n&l;/p&g;\n&l;strong&g;Online and Technology Business Prices&l;/strong&g;&l;br&g;\n&l;table&g;\n&l;tbody&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;&l;u&g;Year Sold&l;/u&g;&a;nbsp;&a;nbsp;&a;nbsp;\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;&l;u&g;Median Asking Price&l;/u&g;&a;nbsp;&a;nbsp;&a;nbsp;\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;&l;u&g;Median Sale Price&l;/u&g;&a;nbsp;&a;nbsp;&a;nbsp;\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;2018\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$489,500\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$470,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;2019\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$550,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$528,464\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;2020\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$650,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$600,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;2021\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$799,500\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$794,500\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;2022\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$590,999\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$550,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;tr&g;\n\t&l;td&g;2023\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$875,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n\t&l;td&g;$850,000\n\t&l;/td&g;\n&l;/tr&g;\n&l;/tbody&g;\n&l;/table&g;\n&l;br&g;\n&l;h3&g;Sell Your Online and Technology Business&l;/h3&g;\n&l;p&g;Knowing the value of your online, technology, and e-commerce business is key to developing a successful exit plan if you’re considering selling it. If you’re looking to sell your e-commerce company, see our Guide, &l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/learning-center/guide/sell-ecommerce-business/\&q;&g;How to Value &a; Sell Your E-Commerce Business&l;/a&g;, to get started. &a;nbsp;\n&l;/p&g;&q;,&q;image1&q;:&q;online-and-technology-businesses-for-sale.jpg&q;,&q;caption1&q;:&q;Own an Online or Technology Business&q;,&q;image2&q;:&q;&q;,&q;caption2&q;:&q;&q;,&q;image3&q;:&q;&q;,&q;caption3&q;:&q;&q;,&q;image4&q;:&q;&q;,&q;caption4&q;:&q;&q;,&q;image1AltText&q;:&q;Buy an Online or Technology Business Today&q;,&q;image2AltText&q;:&q;&q;,&q;image3AltText&q;:&q;&q;,&q;pageH1&q;:&q;&q;,&q;pageMetaDescription&q;:&q;Browse through Online and Technology Businesses currently available for sale on BizBuySell. View e-commerce-related businesses in a wide-variety of sectors to find the right opportunity for you!&q;,&q;pageTitle&q;:&q;&q;,&q;tabTitle&q;:&q;&q;,&q;sources&q;:&q;&l;ul&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/insight-report/\&q;&g;BizBuySell Insight Report&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n\t&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.bizbuysell.com/learning-center/industry-valuation-multiples/\&q;&g;Business Valuation Multiples&l;/a&g;&a;nbsp;&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;&q;,&q;image4AltText&q;:&q;&q;,&q;Dnntags&q;:[&q;BBS_-623953752&q;]}},&q;message&q;:null}}</script>
</div>
